  <span m='1693010'>which</span> <span m='1693250'>are</span> <span m='1694420'>basically</span>
  <span m='1694900'>the</span> <span m='1695140'>most</span> <span m='1695500'>fundamental</span>
  <span m='1696130'>basic</span> <span m='1696490'>thing</span> <span m='1697450'>we</span>
  <span m='1697600'>use</span> <span m='1698020'>in</span> <span m='1698170'>these</span>
  <span m='1698350'>systems.</span> </p><p><span m='1698980'>And</span> <span m='1699490'>I</span>

  <span m='1708400'>extremely</span> <span m='1708760'>powerful.</span> <span m='1709460'>The</span>

  <span m='1717340'>bunch</span> <span m='1717550'>of</span> <span m='1717670'>ones</span>

  </p><p><span m='1787770'>OK.</span> <span m='1787960'>So</span> <span m='1789070'>this</span>

  <span m='1858840'>the</span> <span m='1858960'>output.</span> <span m='1860250'>So</span>
  <span m='1860670'>even</span> <span m='1861000'>though</span> <span m='1861150'>you</span>

  <span m='1867900'>dissimilar,</span> <span m='1868350'>as</span> <span m='1868470'>in</span>
  <span m='1868560'>about</span> <span m='1868770'>half</span> <span m='1868980'>the</span>
  <span m='1869070'>output</span> <span m='1869310'>changed.</span> <span m='1869910'>If</span>
  <span m='1870180'>every</span> <span m='1870510'>bit</span> <span m='1870690'>changes,</span>

  <span m='1879270'>where</span> <span m='1880170'>generally</span> <span m='1880560'>they're</span>
  <span m='1880950'>iterative</span> <span m='1881490'>rounds.</span> <span m='1882180'>And</span>
  <span m='1882270'>so</span> <span m='1882360'>you</span> <span m='1882420'>say,</span>
  <span m='1882570'>OK,</span> <span m='1882780'>I'm</span> <span m='1882870'>going</span>
  <span m='1882990'>to</span> <span m='1883260'>swap</span> <span m='1883620'>these</span>
  <span m='1883830'>things</span> <span m='1884220'>and</span> <span m='1884310'>multiply</span>
  <span m='1884700'>these</span> <span m='1884910'>things</span> <span m='1885210'>and</span>
  <span m='1885300'>shift</span> <span m='1885510'>these</span> <span m='1885750'>bits</span>
  <span m='1885990'>around</span> <span m='1887040'>such</span> <span m='1887340'>that</span>
  <span m='1887550'>if</span> <span m='1887790'>any</span> <span m='1888270'>change</span>
  <span m='1888840'>in</span> <span m='1888990'>the</span> <span m='1889260'>beginning</span>

  <span m='3177500'>And</span> <span m='3177910'>this</span> <span m='3178090'>applies</span>

  <span m='3179200'>going</span> <span m='3179410'>to</span> <span m='3179500'>talk</span>
  <span m='3179710'>about</span> <span m='3179950'>a</span> <span m='3180010'>hash-based</span>
  <span m='3180670'>signature</span> <span m='3181600'>in</span> <span m='3181720'>detail,</span>
  <span m='3183160'>but</span> <span m='3183340'>there</span> <span m='3183490'>are</span>
  <span m='3183550'>many</span> <span m='3183910'>different</span> <span m='3184240'>signature</span>

  <span m='3190540'>curve</span> <span m='3190840'>signatures.</span> <span m='3191860'>There's</span>
  <span m='3192430'>tons</span> <span m='3193030'>of</span> <span m='3193150'>different</span>
  <span m='3193630'>cool</span> <span m='3194110'>math</span> <span m='3194500'>systems</span>
  <span m='3195470'>that</span> <span m='3196120'>allow</span> <span m='3196880'>these</span>
  <span m='3197440'>kinds</span> <span m='3197680'>of</span> <span m='3197740'>functions.</span>
  <span m='3199450'>And</span> <span m='3199600'>I'll</span> <span m='3199690'>talk</span>
  <span m='3199900'>about</span> <span m='3200470'>in</span> <span m='3200620'>some</span>
  <span m='3200770'>ways,</span> <span m='3200950'>this is</span> <span m='3201300'>one</span>
  <span m='3201490'>of</span> <span m='3201550'>the</span> <span m='3201610'>simplest</span>
  <span m='3202000'>ones.</span> </p><p><span m='3203520'>So</span> <span m='3203710'>yeah,</span>
  <span m='3204010'>there's</span> <span m='3204190'>these</span> <span m='3204340'>three</span>
  <span m='3204490'>functions.</span> <span m='3205070'>The</span> <span m='3205170'>first</span>
  <span m='3205270'>one</span> <span m='3205390'>is</span> <span m='3205510'>generate</span>
  <span m='3205840'>keys.</span> <span m='3206690'>And</span> <span m='3206740'>it</span>
  <span m='3206800'>returns</span> <span m='3207430'>a</span> <span m='3207520'>private</span>

  <span m='3210500'>generally</span> <span m='3210730'>doesn't</span> <span m='3210970'>take</span>
  <span m='3211180'>any</span> <span m='3211330'>arguments,</span> <span m='3212500'>but</span>
  <span m='3212800'>it</span> <span m='3212920'>takes</span> <span m='3213160'>in</span>
  <span m='3213430'>randomness.</span> <span m='3214030'>You</span> <span m='3214120'>need</span>
  <span m='3214270'>to</span> <span m='3214360'>flip</span> <span m='3214600'>coins.</span>
  <span m='3215020'>You</span> <span m='3215080'>need</span> <span m='3215230'>to</span>

  <span m='3218710'>long</span> <span m='3219010'>enough</span> <span m='3219250'>that</span>

  <span m='3395050'>about</span> <span m='3395290'>this</span> <span m='3396010'>late</span>
